<h1 _ngcontent-hkt-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="Text"> Text </h1>

<div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>显示一段文本的组件。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>该组件从API version 7开始支持。后续版本如有新增内容，则采用上角标单独标记该内容的起始版本。</p>      <p>文本在组件区域显示效果与字体资源相关，默认字体排印可见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/design-guides/font-0000001828772001" target="_blank">字体排印视觉指引</a>。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 274px;">     <h2 id="子组件" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">子组件<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="子组件" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>可以包含<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-span">Span</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-imagespan">ImageSpan</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-symbolspan">SymbolSpan</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-containerspan">ContainerSpan</a>子组件。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#子组件">子组件</a>实现<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-text-image-layout" target="_blank">图文混排</a>场景。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 690px;">     <h2 id="接口" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">接口<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="接口" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Text(content?: string | Resource , value?: TextOptions)</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">content</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resource">Resource</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本内容。当不包含子组件<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-span">Span</a>和未设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-styled-string">属性字符串</a>时该参数生效。</p>          <p>默认值：' '</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>显示内容的优先级：属性字符串&gt;Span&gt;Text的文本内容。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value<sup>11+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a width="25%">文本组件初始化选项。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3993px;">     <h2 </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 669px;">     <h3 id="baselineoffset" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">baselineOffset<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="baselineoffset" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>baselineOffset(value: number | ResourceStr)</p>     <p>设置文本基线的偏移量。</p>     <p>设置该值为百分比时，按默认值显示。</p>     <p>正数内容向上偏移，负数向下偏移。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.10.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | <a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#resourcestr">ResourceStr</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本基线的偏移量。</p>          <p>默认值：0</p>          <p>从API version 20开始，支持Resource类型。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1032px;">     <h3 id="bindselectionmenu11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">bindSelectionMenu<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="bindselectionmenu11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>bindSelectionMenu(spanType: TextSpanType, content: CustomBuilder, responseType: TextResponseType,</p>     <p>options?: SelectionMenuOptions)</p>     <p>设置自定义选择菜单。</p>     <p>bindSelectionMenu的长按响应时长为600ms，bindContextMenu的长按响应时长为800ms，当两者同时绑定且触发方式均为长按时，优先响应bindSelectionMenu。</p>     <p>自定义菜单超长时，建议内部嵌套使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-scroll">Scroll</a>组件，避免键盘被遮挡。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口不支持在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-attribute-modifier#attributemodifier">attributeModifier</a>中调用。</p>       <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#editmenuoptions12">editMenuOptions</a>设置文本选择菜单时，保留系统默认的风格，触发菜单弹出的条件不变。</p>       <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#bindselectionmenu11">bindSelectionMenu</a>设置文本选择菜单时，风格由开发者定义，触发菜单弹出的条件由开发者定义。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.11.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">选择菜单的选项。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 493px;">     <h3 id="caretcolor14" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">caretColor<sup>14+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="caretcolor14" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span <h3 id="copyoption9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">copyOption<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="copyoption9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>copyOption(value: CopyOptions)</p>     <p>设置组件是否支持文本可复制粘贴。</p>     <p>从API version 20开始，当Text组件执行复制操作时，会将HTML格式的内容添加到剪贴板中。</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>当Text组件包含子组件时，仅支持<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-span">Span</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-imagespan">ImageSpan</a>子组件向剪贴板中添加HTML格式的内容。</p></li>      <li>       <p>设置Text组件的属性字符串时，请参考属性字符串<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-styled-string#tohtml14">toHtml</a>接口文档，以了解支持转换为HTML的范围。</p></li>     </ul>     <p>设置copyOption为CopyOptions.InApp或者CopyOptions.LocalDevice时：</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>长按文本，会弹出文本选择菜单，可选中文本并进行复制、全选操作。</p></li>      <li>       <p>默认情况下，长按选中文本可拖拽。若要取消此功能，可将 draggable 设置为 false。</p></li>      <li>       <p>若需要支持Ctrl+C复制，需同时设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textselectable12">textSelectable</a>为TextSelectableMode.SELECTABLE_FOCUSABLE。</p></li>     </ul>     <p>此时Text会监听onClick事件，手势事件为非冒泡事件，若需要点击Text组件区域响应父组件的点击手势事件，建议在父组件上使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-gesture-settings#parallelgesture">parallelGesture</a>绑定手势识别，也可参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#示例7设置文本识别">示例7设置文本识别</a>。</p>     <p>由于卡片没有长按事件，此场景下长按文本，不会弹出文本选择菜单。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.14.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.14.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.14.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.14.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#copyoptions9">CopyOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>组件是否支持文本可复制粘贴。</p>          <p>默认值：CopyOptions.None</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 517px;">     <h3 id="datadetectorconfig11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">dataDetectorConfig<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="datadetectorconfig11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div <p>设置文本识别配置，可配置识别类型、实体显示样式，以及是否开启长按预览等。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#enabledatadetector11">enableDataDetector</a>一起使用，设置enableDataDetector为true时，dataDetectorConfig的配置才能生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 921px;">     <h3 id="decoration" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">decoration<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="decoration" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>decoration(value: DecorationStyleInterface)</p>     <p>设置文本装饰线样式及其颜色。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当文字的下边缘轮廓与装饰线位置相交时，会触发下划线避让规则，下划线将在这些字符处避让文字。常见“gjyqp”等英文字符。</p>       <p>当文本装饰线的颜色设置为Color.Transparent时，装饰线颜色设置为跟随每行第一个字的字体颜色。当文本装饰线的颜色设置为透明色16进制对应值“#00FFFFFF”时，装饰线颜色设置为透明色。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本装饰线样式对象。</p>          <p>默认值：</p>          <p>{</p>          <p>type: TextDecorationType.None,</p>          <p>color: Color.Black,</p>          <p>style: TextDecorationStyle.SOLID</p>          <p>}</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>style参数不支持卡片能力。</p></td>        </tr> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">draggable<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="draggable9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>draggable(value: boolean)</p>     <p>设置选中文本拖拽效果。</p>     <p>不能和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-events-drag-drop#ondragstart">onDragStart</a>事件同时使用。</p>     <p>当draggable设置为true时，需配合<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#copyoptions9">CopyOptions</a>使用，设置copyOptions为CopyOptions.InApp或者CopyOptions.LocalDevice，支持对选中文本的拖拽及复制到输入框。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.13.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"   <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 657px;">     <h3 id="editmenuoptions12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">editMenuOptions<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="editmenuoptions12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>editMenuOptions(editMenu: EditMenuOptions)</p>     <p>设置自定义菜单扩展项，允许用户设置扩展项的文本内容、图标、回调方法。</p>     <p>调用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-textmenucontroller#disablemenuitems20">disableMenuItems</a>或<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-uicontext-textmenucontroller#disablesystemservicemenuitems20">disableSystemServiceMenuItems</a>接口屏蔽文本选择菜单内的系统服务菜单项时，editMenuOptions接口内回调方法<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#oncreatemenu12">onCreateMenu</a>的入参列表中不包含被屏蔽的菜单选项。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#editmenuoptions12">editMenuOptions</a>设置文本选择菜单时，保留系统默认的风格，触发菜单弹出的条件不变。</p>       <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#bindselectionmenu11">bindSelectionMenu</a>设置文本选择菜单时，风格由开发者定义，触发菜单弹出的条件由开发者定义。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">     <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">扩展菜单选项。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 589px;"> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">enableDataDetector<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="enabledatadetector11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>enableDataDetector(enable: boolean)</p>     <p>设置是否进行文本特殊实体识别。</p>     <p>该接口依赖设备底层应具有文本识别能力，否则设置不会生效。</p>     <p>当enableDataDetector设置为true，同时不设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#datadetectorconfig11">dataDetectorConfig</a>属性时，默认识别所有类型的实体，所识别实体的样式如下，即字体颜色改为蓝色、并添加蓝色下划线。</p>     <div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-hkt-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'#ff007dff'</span></li><li><span class="hljs-attr">decoration</span>:{</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">TextDecorationType</span>.<span class="hljs-property">Underline</span>,</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">color</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'#ff007dff'</span>,</li><li>  <span class="hljs-attr">style</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">TextDecorationStyle</span>.<span class="hljs-property">SOLID</span></li><li>}</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p>触摸点击和鼠标右键点击实体，会根据实体类型弹出对应的实体操作菜单，鼠标左键点击实体会直接响应菜单的第一个选项。</p>     <p>当overflow设置为TextOverflow.MARQUEE时，该功能不会生效。</p>     <p>当copyOption设置为CopyOptions.None时，点击实体弹出的菜单不包含选择文本、复制、翻译、分享和搜索功能。当copyOption不为CopyOptions.None，且textSelectable设置为TextSelectableMode.UNSELECTABLE时，仍然具有实体复制功能，但不包含选择文本功能。</p>     <p>从API version 20开始，支持选中文本后，在文本选择菜单与鼠标右键菜单中显示实体识别选项。当enableDataDetector设置为true，且<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#copyoption9">copyOption</a>设置为CopyOptions.LocalDevice或CopyOptions.CROSS_DEVICE时，该功能生效。菜单选项包括<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#textmenuitemid12">TextMenuItemId</a>中的url（打开链接）、email（新建邮件）、phoneNumber（呼叫）、address（导航至该位置）、dateTime（新建日程提醒）。</p>     <p>AI菜单生效时，需选中范围内，包括一个完整的AI实体，才能展示对应的选项。</p>     <p>从API version 20开始，支持选中文本后，在文本选择菜单与鼠标右键菜单中显示问问小艺选项。当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#copyoption9">copyOption</a>设置为CopyOptions.LocalDevice或CopyOptions.CROSS_DEVICE时，若enableDataDetector设置为false，显示问问小艺选项。若enableDataDetector设置为true，此时选中范围内，没有包括一个完整的AI实体或包括超过一个完整的AI实体，才能展示对应的选项。相关选项为<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#textmenuitemid12">TextMenuItemId</a>中的askAI（问问小艺）。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead> </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 729px;">     <h3 id="fontfamily" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fontFamily<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>可以使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-graphics-text#loadfontsync">loadFontSync</a>注册自定义字体。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1951px;">     <h3 id="fontfeature12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fontFeature<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fontfeature12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>fontFeature(value: string)</p>     <p>设置文字特性效果，比如数字等宽的特性。</p>     <p>格式为：normal | &lt;feature-tag-value&gt;</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的格式为：&lt;string&gt; [ &lt;integer&gt; | on | off ]</p>     <p>&lt;feature-tag-value&gt;的个数可以有多个，中间用','隔开。</p>     <p>例如，使用等宽数字的输入格式为："ss01" on。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>不支持Text内同时存在文本内容和Span或ImageSpan子组件。如果同时存在，只显示Span或ImageSpan内的内容。</p>       <p>字体排版引擎会对开发者传入的宽度<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#width">width</a>进行向下取整，保证是整型像素后进行排版。如果向上取整，可能会出现文字右侧被截断。</p>       <p>当多个Text组件在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-container-row">Row</a>容器内布局且没有设置具体的布局分配信息时，Text会以Row的最大尺寸进行布局。如果需要子组件主轴累加的尺寸不超过Row容器主轴的尺寸，可以设置<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-size#layoutweight">layoutWeight</a>或者是以<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-flex-layout">Flex</a>布局来约束子组件的主轴尺寸。</p>       <p>系统默认字体支持的liga连字：Th fb ff fb ffb ffh ffi ffk ffl fh fi fk fl rf rt rv rx ry。常导致Span、属性字符串的效果不符合预期，关闭liga连字特性可以规避。</p>       <p>文字特性效果与使用的字体文件密切相关。例如，8标点挤压功能在当前系统默认字体中仅对左侧标点符号生效，而右侧标点符号及感叹号、顿号、问号均不生效。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.13.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.13.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.13.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.23.13.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">文字特性效果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>fontFeature属性列表：</p>     <p><span><img originheight="766" originwidth="594" src="https://alliance-communityfile-drcn.dbankcdn.com/FileServer/getFile/cmtyPub/011/111/111/0000000000011111111.20251211115414.07576015232584538048277124005926:50001231000000:2800:E0AFEAAB81925AA982BC5ECED971FEB03595A631C2B53BECC26AFA3A90E2150A.png" width="594" height="766"></span></p>     <p>设置fontFeature属性，fontFeature是OpenType字体的高级排版能力，如支持连字、数字等宽等特性，一般用在自定义字体中，其能力需要字体本身支持。</p>     <p>更多fontFeature能力介绍可参考<a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-feature-settings-prop" target="_blank">font-feature-settings property</a>和<a href="https://sparanoid.com/lab/opentype-features/" target="_blank">OpenType Features</a>。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 661px;">     <h3 id="fontsize" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fontSize<i class="anchor-icon style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1210px;">     <h3 id="fontweight12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">fontWeight<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="fontweight12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>fontWeight(weight: number | FontWeight | ResourceStr, options?: FontSettingOptions)</p>     <p>设置文本字重，支持设置字体配置项。</p>     <p>仅Text组件生效，其子组件不生效。常见问题参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-text-faq#设置enablevariablefontweight为true后字重不能跟随设置调节" target="_blank">设置enableVariableFontWeight为true后字重不能跟随设置调节</a>。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.27.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>  <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置字体配置项。</p>          <p>当options的参数enableVariableFontWeight取值false时，禁用可变字重调节，weight取值为[100, 900]范围内的整百数值时，字重取值为weight。weight是非整百数值时，字重取默认值400。</p>          <p>当options的参数enableVariableFontWeight取值true时，启用可变字重调节，weight取值为[100, 900]范围内任意整数时，字重取值为weight。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div       <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.28.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">halfLeading</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>设置文本是否垂直居中。</p>          <p>true表示将行间距平分至行的顶部与底部，false则不平分。</p>          <p>默认值：false</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 821px;">     <h3 id="heightadaptivepolicy10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">heightAdaptivePolicy<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="heightadaptivepolicy10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>heightAdaptivePolicy(value: TextHeightAdaptivePolicy)</p>     <p>设置文本自适应布局调整字号的方式。</p>     <p>规则如下：</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>MAX_LINES_FIRST模式：优先使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#maxlines">maxLines</a>属性来调整文本高度。如果使用maxLines属性的布局大小超过了布局约束，则尝试在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#minfontsize">minFontSize</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#maxfontsize">maxFontSize</a>的范围内缩小字体以显示更多文本。</p></li>      <li>       <p>MIN_FONT_SIZE_FIRST模式：优先使用minFontSize属性来调整文本高度。如果使用minFontSize属性可以将文本布局在一行中，则尝试在minFontSize和maxFontSize的范围内增大字体并使用最大可能的字体大小在一行内显示，否则按minFontSize显示。</p></li>      <li>       <p>LAYOUT_CONSTRAINT_FIRST模式：优先使用布局约束来调整文本高度。如果布局大小超过布局约束，则尝试在minFontSize和maxFontSize的范围内缩小字体以满足布局约束。如果将字体大小缩小到minFontSize后，布局大小仍然超过布局约束，则删除超过布局约束的行。</p></li>     </ul>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.29.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textheightadaptivepolicy10">TextHeightAdaptivePolicy</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本自适应高度的方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextHeightAdaptivePolicy.MAX_LINES_FIRST</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 781px;">     <h3 id="letterspacing" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">letterSpacing<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="letterspacing" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>letterSpacing(value: number | ResourceStr)</p>     <p>设置文本字符间距。</p>     <p>设置该值为百分比时，按默认值显示。设置该值为0时，按默认值显示。string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>当取值为负值时，文字会被压缩。负值过小时会将组件内容区大小压缩为0，导致内容无法显示。</p>     <p>对每个字符生效，包括行尾字符。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p> class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>maxFontSize(value: number | string | Resource)</p>     <p>设置文本最大显示字号。</p>     <p>string类型支持number类型取值的字符串形式，可以附带单位，例如"10"、"10fp"。</p>     <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#minfontsize">minFontSize</a>以及<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#maxlines">maxLines</a>或布局大小限制使用，单独设置不生效。</p>     <p>自适应字号生效时，fontSize设置不生效。</p>     <p>maxFontSize小于等于0或者maxFontSize小于minFontSize时，自适应字号不生效，此时按照<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#fontsize">fontSize</a>属性的值生效，未设置时按照其默认值生效。</p>     <p>从API version 18开始支持在子组件和属性字符串上生效，未设置字号的部分会自适应。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.13.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.37.13.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number | string | <a width="25%">          <p>文本最大显示字号。</p>          <p>单位：<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-pixel-units">fp</a></p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 685px;">     <h3 id="maxlines" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">maxLines<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="maxlines" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span <p>默认情况下，文本是自动折行的，如果指定此属性，则文本最多不会超过指定的行。如果有多余的文本，可以通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textoverflow">textOverflow</a>来指定截断方式。</p>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p> version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">optimizeTrailingSpace<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="optimizetrailingspace20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>optimizeTrailingSpace(optimize: Optional&lt;boolean&gt;)</p>     <p>设置是否在文本布局过程中优化每行末尾的空格，可解决行尾空格影响对齐显示效果问题。</p>     <p>设置Text.optimizeTrailingSpace为true时：</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>多行、单行、图文混排等多种情况下均会优化行尾空格（TextAlign.Center或TextAlign.End时，优化效果明显）；</p></li>      <li>       <p>纯空格文本时，修饰线、阴影、背景色跟随空格文本显示；</p></li>      <li>       <p>行首空格不在优化范围内，行尾文本强制换行，每行行尾空格根据组件宽度优化行尾空格。</p></li>     </ul>     <p>当纯空格文本设置优化行尾空格<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#optimizetrailingspace20">optimizeTrailingSpace</a>为true时，不允许同时设置文本背景色<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-background#backgroundcolor">backgroundColor</a>、空格装饰线<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#decoration">decoration</a>和对齐<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textalign">textAlign</a>三个属性。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.10.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.41.10.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"     <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">optimize</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 874px;">     <h3 id="selection11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">selection<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="selection11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>selection(selectionStart: number, selectionEnd: number)</p>     <p>设置选中区域。</p>     <p>选中区域高亮且显示手柄和文本选择菜单。</p>     <p>当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#copyoption9">copyOption</a>设置为CopyOptions.None时，设置selection属性不生效。</p>     <p>当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textoverflow">textOverflow</a>设置为TextOverflow.MARQUEE时，设置selection属性不生效。</p>     <p>当selectionStart大于等于selectionEnd时不选中。可选范围为[0, textSize]，其中textSize为文本内容最大字符数，入参小于0时处理为0，大于textSize时处理为textSize。</p>     <p>当selectionStart或selectionEnd位于截断的不可见区域时，文本不选中。当<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-sharp-clipping#clip12">clip</a>设置为false时，超出父组件的文本可以被选中。</p>     <p>可通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#ontextselectionchange11">onTextSelectionChange</a>接口获取选中区域位置变化结果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.13.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.13.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.13.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.44.13.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">selectionStart</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>所选文本的起始位置。</p>          <p>默认值：-1</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">selectionEnd</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>所选文本的结束位置。</p>          <p>默认值：-1</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 877px;">     <h3 id="shaderstyle20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">shaderStyle<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="shaderstyle20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>shaderStyle(shader: ShaderStyle)</p>     <p>可以显示为径向渐变<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#radialgradientstyle20">RadialGradientStyle</a>或线性渐变<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#lineargradientstyle20">LinearGradientStyle</a>或纯色<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#colorshaderstyle20">ColorShaderStyle</a>的效果，shaderStyle的优先级高于<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-symbolspan#fontcolor">fontColor</a>和AI识别，纯色建议使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-symbolspan#fontcolor">fontColor</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">shader</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#shaderstyle20">ShaderStyle</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>径向渐变或线性渐变或纯色。</p>          <p>根据传入的参数区分处理径向渐变<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#radialgradientstyle20">RadialGradientStyle</a>或线性渐变<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#lineargradientstyle20">LinearGradientStyle</a>或纯色<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#colorshaderstyle20">ColorShaderStyle</a>，最终设置到Text文本上显示为渐变色效果。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>当设置为径向渐变<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-text-common#radialgradientstyle20">RadialGradientStyle</a>时，若<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-gradient-color#radialgradientoptions18对象说明">RadialGradientOptions</a>的center参数设置到组件范围外时，可将repeating参数设置为true，此时渐变效果会更明显。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1009px;">     <h3 id="textalign" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textAlign<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textalign" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textAlign(value: TextAlign)</p>     <p>设置文本段落在水平方向的对齐方式。</p>     <p>文本段落宽度占满Text组件宽度。</p>     <p>可通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-location#align">align</a>属性控制文本段落在垂直方向上的位置，此组件中不可通过align属性控制文本段落在水平方向上的位置，具体效果如下：</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>Alignment.TopStart、Alignment.Top、Alignment.TopEnd：内容顶部对齐。</p></li>      <li>       <p>Alignment.Start、Alignment.Center、Alignment.End：内容垂直居中。</p></li>      <li>       <p>Alignment.BottomStart、Alignment.Bottom、Alignment.BottomEnd：内容底部对齐。</p></li>     </ul>     <p>当textAlign属性设置为TextAlign.JUSTIFY时，需要根据文本内容设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#wordbreak11">wordBreak</a>属性，且最后一行文本水平对齐首部，不参与两端对齐。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>textAlign只能调整文本整体的布局，不影响字符的显示顺序。若需要调整字符的显示顺序，请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-internationalization#镜像状态字符对齐" target="_blank">镜像状态字符对齐</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.13.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.13.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.13.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.46.13.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-appendix-enums#textalign">TextAlign</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本段落在水平方向的对齐方式。</p>          <p>默认值：TextAlign.Start</p>          <p>Wearable设备上默认值为：TextAlign.Center</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 541px;">     <h3 id="textcase" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textCase<i <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.47.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>文本大小写。</p>          <p>默认值：TextCase.Normal</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="textcontentalign21" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textContentAlign<sup>21+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon <p>此接口可以在文本内容区高度大于组件高度时生效，确保文本内容区的对齐方式正确显示。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 21开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">textContentAlign</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-custom-property#optionalt12">Optional</a>&lt;<a </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 493px;">     <h3 id="textindent10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textIndent<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textindent10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textIndent(value: Length)</p>     <p>设置首行文本缩进。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-types#length">Length</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>首行文本缩进。</p>          <p>默认值：0</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1101px;">     <h3 id="textoverflow" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textOverflow<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textoverflow" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>textOverflow(options: TextOverflowOptions)</p>     <p>设置文本超长时的显示方式。</p>     <p>当<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textoverflowoptions18对象说明">TextOverflowOptions</a>设置为TextOverflow.None、TextOverflow.Clip或TextOverflow.Ellipsis时：</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>设置为TextOverflow.None、TextOverflow.Clip，文本超长时按最大行截断显示。</p></li>      <li>       <p>设置为TextOverflow.Ellipsis，文本超长时显示不下的文本用省略号代替。</p></li>      <li>       <p>需配合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#maxlines">maxLines</a>使用，单独设置不生效。</p></li>      <li>       <p>断行规则参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#wordbreak11">wordBreak</a>。默认情况下参考WordBreak.BREAK_WORD的截断方式，文本截断按字进行。例如，英文以单词为最小单位进行截断。若需要以字母为单位进行截断，可设置wordBreak属性为WordBreak.BREAK_ALL。</p></li>      <li>       <p>折行规则参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#linebreakstrategy12">lineBreakStrategy</a>。该属性在<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#wordbreak11">wordBreak</a>不等于WordBreak.BREAK_ALL的时候生效，不支持连词符。</p></li>      <li>       <p>从API version 11开始，建议优先组合<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textoverflow">textOverflow</a>和<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#wordbreak11">wordBreak</a>属性来设置截断方式，具体详见<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#示例4设置文本断行及折行">示例4设置文本断行及折行</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-faqs/faqs-arkui-347" target="_blank">如何解决Text组件文本为中文、数字、英文混合时显示省略号截断异常的问题</a>。</p></li>     </ul>     <p>当TextOverflowOptions设置为TextOverflow.MARQUEE时：</p>     <ul>      <li>       <p>文本在一行内滚动显示。</p></li>      <li>       <p>设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#maxlines">maxLines</a>及<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#copyoption9">copyOption</a>属性均不生效。</p></li>      <li>       <p>Text组件<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-sharp-clipping#clip12">clip</a>属性默认为true。</p></li>      <li>       <p>属性字符串的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-styled-string#customspan">CustomSpan</a>不支持跑马灯模式。</p></li>      <li>       <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textalign">textAlign</a>属性的生效规则：当文本不可滚动时，textAlign属性生效；当文本可滚动时，textAlign属性不生效。</p></li>      <li>       <p>从API version 12开始，当TextOverflowOptions设置为TextOverflow.MARQUEE时，支持ImageSpan组件，文本和图片可在一行内滚动显示。</p></li>     </ul>     <p><strong>卡片能力：</strong> 从API version 9开始，该接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.12.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.12.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.12.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.50.12.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#textoverflowoptions18对象说明">TextOverflowOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">文本超长显示方式对象</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 613px;">     <h3 id="textselectable12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">textSelectable<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="textselectable12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#copyoption9">copyOption</a>使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.51.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">mode</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 661px;">     <h3 id="wordbreak11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">wordBreak<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="wordbreak11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>wordBreak(value: WordBreak)</p>     <p>设置断行规则。</p>     <p>默认情况下，不调用wordBreak或者设置WordBreak.BREAK_WORD时，文本截断按字进行。例如，英文以单词为最小单位进行截断。</p>     <p>WordBreak.BREAK_ALL与{overflow: TextOverflow.Ellipsis}、maxLines组合使用，可实现英文单词按字母截断，超出部分以省略号显示。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder"> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>断行规则。</p>          <p>默认值：WordBreak.BREAK_WORD</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>菜单类型的匹配顺序如下。例如，用户长按文本时，根据以下规则查找：</p>       <ol>        <li>查找是否注册了TextSpanType.TEXT、TextResponseType.LONG_PRESS菜单</li>        <li>查找是否注册了TextSpanType.TEXT、TextResponseType.DEFAULT菜单</li>        <li>查找是否注册了TextSpanType.DEFAULT、TextResponseType.LONG_PRESS菜单</li>        <li>查找是否注册了TextSpanType.DEFAULT、TextResponseType.DEFAULT菜单</li>       </ol>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 992px;">     <h2 class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 453px;">     <h3 id="oncopy11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">onCopy<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon id="setstyledstring12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setStyledString<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setstyledstring12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setStyledString(value: StyledString): void</p>     <p>触发绑定或更新属性字符串。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.66.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.66.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.66.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.66.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-styled-string#styledstring">StyledString</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>属性字符串。</p>          <p><strong>说明：</strong></p>          <p>StyledString的子类<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-styled-string#mutablestyledstring">MutableStyledString</a>也可以作为入参值。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>多次调用setStyledString，会用新的入参覆盖已绑定的属性字符串，而不是叠加新的入参。</p>       <p>属性字符串通过controller绑定时，需要等待布局完成后，绑定生效。当<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-framenode#measure12">measure</a>和setStyledString同时使用，开发者需要通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkui-inspector">@ohos.arkui.inspector (布局回调)</a>判断布局完成，再绑定属性字符串。</p>       <p>在API version 14及以下版本，开发者调用TextController的setStyledString接口设置属性字符串，如果调用时TextController还未绑定对应的Text，则此次设置无效。</p>       <p>从API version 15开始，TextController会保存设置的属性字符串。当TextController已经和Text绑定，则Text会自动设置属性字符串，显示对应的样式。</p>       <p>这一区别体现在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-custom-component-lifecycle#abouttoappear">aboutToAppear</a>中设置属性字符串，API 14及以下版本不生效，API 15及以上版本生效，推荐用法请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/arkts-styled-string#创建并应用styledstring和mutablestyledstring" target="_blank">创建并应用StyledString和MutableStyledString</a>。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 489px;">     <h3 id="getlayoutmanager12" </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 495px;">     <h2 id="marqueestate18枚举说明" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">MarqueeState<sup>18+</sup>枚举说明<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="marqueestate18枚举说明" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>Marquee状态回调的返回值。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 18开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.ArkUI.ArkUI.Full</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.70.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.70.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.70.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">START</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">跑马灯滚动开始。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">BOUNCE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">完成一次跑马灯滚动，如果循环次数不是1，将会多次返回。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">FINISH</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" anchorid="示例7设置文本识别" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <p>从API version 11开始，该示例通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#enabledatadetector11">enableDataDetector</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#enabledatadetector11">enableDataDetector</a>设为true且不设置<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-basic-components-text#datadetectorconfig11">dataDetectorConfig</a>时，系统会识别所有实体类型，并将识别实体的字体颜色改为蓝色、添加蓝色下划线。</p>     <div _ngcontent-hkt-c106=""
